// PATTERN \u{2014} apply to ALL repos where GetAllAsync returns empty:
// CategoryRepository.cs:
public async Task<IEnumerable<Category>> GetAllAsync()
{
    await using var conn = await _factory.CreateConnectionAsync();
    await using var cmd  = conn.CreateCommand();
    cmd.CommandText = "SELECT * FROM Categories ORDER BY name";
    await using var r = await cmd.ExecuteReaderAsync();
    var list = new List<Category>();
    while (await r.ReadAsync())
        list.Add(new Category
        {
            CategoryId = (int)r.GetInt64(r.GetOrdinal("category_id")),
            Name       = r.GetString(r.GetOrdinal("name")),
            Type       = r.GetString(r.GetOrdinal("type")),
        });
    return list;
}

// FBRepository.GetMenuAsync(bool includeInhouse):
public async Task<IEnumerable<FB>> GetMenuAsync(bool includeInhouse = false)
{
    await using var conn = await _factory.CreateConnectionAsync();
    await using var cmd  = conn.CreateCommand();
    cmd.CommandText = includeInhouse
        ? "SELECT * FROM FBs WHERE type != 'FRESH_RAW' AND is_visible = 1"
        : "SELECT * FROM FBs WHERE type = 'REGULAR' AND is_visible = 1";
    await using var r = await cmd.ExecuteReaderAsync();
    var list = new List<FB>();
    while (await r.ReadAsync())
        list.Add(new FB
        {
            ItemId     = (int)r.GetInt64(r.GetOrdinal("fb_id")),
            Name       = r.GetString(r.GetOrdinal("name")),
            Price      = r.GetDecimal(r.GetOrdinal("price")),
            Type       = Enum.Parse<FBType>(r.GetString(r.GetOrdinal("type"))),
            CategoryId = (int)r.GetInt64(r.GetOrdinal("category_id")),
            IsVisible  = r.GetBoolean(r.GetOrdinal("is_visible")),
            Unit       = r.IsDBNull(r.GetOrdinal("unit")) ? null : r.GetString(r.GetOrdinal("unit")),
        });
    return list;
}

// RestaurantTableRepository.GetAllAsync():
public async Task<IEnumerable<RestaurantTable>> GetAllAsync()
{
    await using var conn = await _factory.CreateConnectionAsync();
    await using var cmd  = conn.CreateCommand();
    cmd.CommandText = "SELECT * FROM RestaurantTables ORDER BY table_id";
    await using var r = await cmd.ExecuteReaderAsync();
    var list = new List<RestaurantTable>();
    while (await r.ReadAsync())
        list.Add(new RestaurantTable
        {
            TableId  = (int)r.GetInt64(r.GetOrdinal("table_id")),
            Status   = Enum.Parse<TableStatus>(r.GetString(r.GetOrdinal("status"))),
            Capacity = r.GetInt32(r.GetOrdinal("capacity")),
        });
    return list;
}

// RestaurantTableRepository.GetByIdAsync(id)  \u{2190} MUST READ FROM DB, not hardcode AVAILABLE:
public async Task<RestaurantTable?> GetByIdAsync(long id)
{
    await using var conn = await _factory.CreateConnectionAsync();
    await using var cmd  = conn.CreateCommand();
    cmd.CommandText = "SELECT * FROM RestaurantTables WHERE table_id = @Id";
    cmd.Parameters.AddWithValue("@Id", id);
    await using var r = await cmd.ExecuteReaderAsync();
    if (!await r.ReadAsync()) return null;
    return new RestaurantTable
    {
        TableId  = (int)r.GetInt64(r.GetOrdinal("table_id")),
        Status   = Enum.Parse<TableStatus>(r.GetString(r.GetOrdinal("status"))),
        Capacity = r.GetInt32(r.GetOrdinal("capacity")),
    };
}

// TableReservationRepository.GetByIdAsync(id) \u{2190} must read DB, currently returns null:
public async Task<TableReservation?> GetByIdAsync(long id)
{
    await using var conn = await _factory.CreateConnectionAsync();
    await using var cmd  = conn.CreateCommand();
    cmd.CommandText = "SELECT * FROM TableReservations WHERE reservation_id = @Id";
    cmd.Parameters.AddWithValue("@Id", id);
    await using var r = await cmd.ExecuteReaderAsync();
    if (!await r.ReadAsync()) return null;
    return new TableReservation
    {
        ReservationId = r.GetInt64(r.GetOrdinal("reservation_id")),
        CustomerId    = r.GetInt64(r.GetOrdinal("customer_id")),
        TableId       = (int)r.GetInt64(r.GetOrdinal("table_id")),
        ReservedAt    = r.GetDateTime(r.GetOrdinal("reserved_at")),
        GuestCount    = r.GetInt32(r.GetOrdinal("guest_count")),
        Notes         = r.IsDBNull(r.GetOrdinal("notes")) ? null : r.GetString(r.GetOrdinal("notes")),
        Status        = Enum.Parse<ReservationStatus>(r.GetString(r.GetOrdinal("status"))),
    };
}

// TableReservationRepository.UpdateStatusAsync() \u{2190} currently a no-op:
public async Task UpdateStatusAsync(long reservationId, ReservationStatus status)
{
    await using var conn = await _factory.CreateConnectionAsync();
    await using var cmd  = conn.CreateCommand();
    cmd.CommandText = "UPDATE TableReservations SET status = @Status WHERE reservation_id = @Id";
    cmd.Parameters.AddWithValue("@Status", status.ToString());
    cmd.Parameters.AddWithValue("@Id", reservationId);
    await cmd.ExecuteNonQueryAsync();
}

// WarehouseRepository.GetReportAsync() \u{2190} currently returns empty:
public async Task<IEnumerable<WarehouseReportRow>> GetReportAsync()
{
    await using var conn = await _factory.CreateConnectionAsync();
    await using var cmd  = conn.CreateCommand();
    cmd.CommandText = @"
        SELECT f.fb_id, f.name, f.type, w.quantity, w.low_stock_threshold,
               CASE WHEN w.quantity = 0 THEN 'OUT_OF_STOCK'
                    WHEN w.quantity <= w.low_stock_threshold THEN 'LOW_STOCK'
                    ELSE 'NORMAL' END AS stock_status
        FROM Warehouses w
        INNER JOIN FBs f ON f.fb_id = w.fb_id
        ORDER BY
            CASE WHEN w.quantity = 0 THEN 0
                 WHEN w.quantity <= w.low_stock_threshold THEN 1 ELSE 2 END, f.name";
    await using var r = await cmd.ExecuteReaderAsync();
    var list = new List<WarehouseReportRow>();
    while (await r.ReadAsync())
        list.Add(new WarehouseReportRow(
            r.GetInt64(0), r.GetString(1),
            Enum.Parse<FBType>(r.GetString(2)),
            r.GetInt32(3), r.GetInt32(4),
            Enum.Parse<StockStatus>(r.GetString(5))));
    return list;
}

// StaffRepository.GetAllAsync():
public async Task<IEnumerable<Staff>> GetAllAsync()
{
    await using var conn = await _factory.CreateConnectionAsync();
    await using var cmd  = conn.CreateCommand();
    cmd.CommandText = "SELECT * FROM Staff ORDER BY full_name";
    await using var r = await cmd.ExecuteReaderAsync();
    var list = new List<Staff>();
    while (await r.ReadAsync())
        list.Add(new Staff
        {
            StaffId  = r.GetInt64(r.GetOrdinal("staff_id")),

// Step 1: Add internal accessor to UnitOfWork:
public class UnitOfWork : IUnitOfWork
{
    internal SqlConnection?    ActiveConnection  => _connection;
    internal SqlTransaction?   ActiveTransaction => _transaction;
    // ... rest unchanged
}

// Step 2: Add BaseRepository that uses UoW's connection when in a transaction:
public abstract class BaseRepository
{
    protected readonly SqlConnectionFactory _factory;
    protected readonly UnitOfWork _uow;

    protected BaseRepository(SqlConnectionFactory factory, UnitOfWork uow)
        => (_factory, _uow) = (factory, uow);

    protected async Task<(SqlConnection conn, SqlTransaction? tx, bool owned)> GetConnAsync()
    {
        if (_uow.ActiveConnection != null)
            // In transaction \u{2014} use shared connection (don't dispose it)
            return (_uow.ActiveConnection, _uow.ActiveTransaction, false);

        var conn = await _factory.CreateConnectionAsync();
        return (conn, null, true);
    }
}

// Step 3: All repos inherit BaseRepository and update every SQL method:
public class OrderItemRepository : BaseRepository, IOrderItemRepository
{
    public OrderItemRepository(SqlConnectionFactory f, UnitOfWork uow) : base(f, uow) {}

    public async Task<long> InsertAndReturnIdAsync(OrderItem item)
    {
        var (conn, tx, owned) = await GetConnAsync();
        try
        {
            await using var cmd = conn.CreateCommand();
            cmd.Transaction = tx;          // \u{2190} attach transaction!
            cmd.CommandText = @"INSERT INTO OrderItems (...) OUTPUT INSERTED.order_item_id VALUES (...)";
            // ... parameters
            return (long)await cmd.ExecuteScalarAsync();
        }
        finally { if (owned) await conn.DisposeAsync(); }
    }
}

// RestaurantOrderRepository.GetAllAsync() \u{2014} implement:
public async Task<IEnumerable<RestaurantOrder>> GetAllAsync()
{
    await using var conn = await _factory.CreateConnectionAsync();
    await using var cmd  = conn.CreateCommand();
    cmd.CommandText = "SELECT * FROM RestaurantOrders ORDER BY created_at DESC";
    await using var r = await cmd.ExecuteReaderAsync();
    var list = new List<RestaurantOrder>();
    while (await r.ReadAsync())
        list.Add(new RestaurantOrder
        {
            OrderId   = r.GetInt64(r.GetOrdinal("order_id")),
            TableId   = (int)r.GetInt64(r.GetOrdinal("table_id")),
            Status    = Enum.Parse<OrderStatus>(r.GetString(r.GetOrdinal("status"))),
            CreatedAt = r.GetDateTime(r.GetOrdinal("created_at")),
        });
    return list;
}

// InvoiceRepository.GetAllAsync() \u{2014} implement:
public async Task<IEnumerable<Invoice>> GetAllAsync()
{
    await using var conn = await _factory.CreateConnectionAsync();
    await using var cmd  = conn.CreateCommand();
    cmd.CommandText = "SELECT * FROM Invoices ORDER BY invoice_id DESC";
    await using var r = await cmd.ExecuteReaderAsync();
    var list = new List<Invoice>();
    while (await r.ReadAsync())
        list.Add(new Invoice
        {
            InvoiceId      = r.GetInt64(r.GetOrdinal("invoice_id")),
            OrderId        = r.GetInt64(r.GetOrdinal("order_id")),
            Subtotal       = r.GetDecimal(r.GetOrdinal("subtotal")),
            DiscountAmount = r.GetDecimal(r.GetOrdinal("discount_amount")),
            Total          = r.GetDecimal(r.GetOrdinal("total")),
            Status         = Enum.Parse<InvoiceStatus>(r.GetString(r.GetOrdinal("status"))),
        });
    return list;
}

// Add GetAllOrdersQuery + Handler:
public record GetAllOrdersQuery() : IRequest<IEnumerable<OrderDto>>;
public class GetAllOrdersQueryHandler : IRequestHandler<GetAllOrdersQuery, IEnumerable<OrderDto>>
{
    private readonly IUnitOfWork _uow;
    public GetAllOrdersQueryHandler(IUnitOfWork uow) => _uow = uow;
    public async Task<IEnumerable<OrderDto>> Handle(GetAllOrdersQuery req, CancellationToken ct)
    {
        var orders = await _uow.Orders.GetAllAsync();
        return orders.Select(o => new OrderDto(o.OrderId, o.TableId, o.Status.ToString(), o.CreatedAt));
    }
}

  'staff-invoices':         () => invoiceService.getAll(),
  'staff-warehouse':        () => warehouseService.getReport(),
  'staff-receipts':         () => receiptService.getAll(),
  'staff-discounts':        () => discountService.getAll(),
  'staff-customers':        () => customerService.getAll(),
  'staff-staff-management': () => staffService.getAll(),
  'staff-reviews':          () => reviewService.getAll(),
  'staff-categories':       () => categoryService.getAll(),
  'staff-manufacturers':    () => manufacturerService.getAll(),
}

async function load() {
  const loader = loaders[pageKey.value]
  if (!loader) { rows.value = []; return; }
  loading.value = true
  try { rows.value = await loader() }
  catch (e: any) { notify.error(e.message ?? 'Failed to load') }
  finally { loading.value = false }
}

const filteredRows = computed(() => {
  const q = query.value.trim().toLowerCase()
  return q ? rows.value.filter(r => JSON.stringify(r).toLowerCase().includes(q)) : rows.value
})

onMounted(load)
watch(pageKey, load)
</script>`})}),(0,o.jsx)(y,{n:2,title:"Fix StaffLoginPage.vue — wrong method name",tag:"frontend/src/pages/staff/StaffLoginPage.vue",children:(0,o.jsx)(d,{c:`

 Next Steps v4 — built by reading the actual source code line by line. 9 sections, 71 checkable tasks. Here's exactly what was found and what to do:

📊 Current State — Scored every endpoint: 10 work with real data, 5 return empty arrays (stubs), 4 have logic gaps. The single biggest problem: every GetAllAsync() returns new List<T>(). Every list page in the staff workspace is blank.
💀 Dead Repos — Per-repo breakdown of which methods are real SQL vs stubs. Critical ones: FBRepository.GetMenuAsync() always empty (menu blank), RestaurantTableRepository.GetByIdAsync() hardcodes AVAILABLE instead of reading DB, TableReservationRepository.GetByIdAsync() always returns null (confirm/cancel crashes), StaffRepository.InsertAndReturnIdAsync() returns hardcoded 1. Exact SQL fix for each.
🔗 UoW Transaction — The UnitOfWork.BeginTransactionAsync() stores _connection+_transaction but every repo calls _factory.CreateConnectionAsync() creating new isolated connections. Transactions do nothing. Exact fix: BaseRepository with GetConnAsync() that uses the shared connection when active.
⚠ Enum Crashes — 4 issues still present: StockStatus has InStock/OutOfStock but SQL returns OUT_OF_STOCK, SqlConnectionFactory has duplicate using System.Data.SqlClient, JWT customer role claim is "Customer" not "CUSTOMER" (causes 403 on all customer endpoints), order flow crashes because Complete() requires SERVING state but no start-serving endpoint exists.
🎨 Design Already Exists — The luxury gold/charcoal design system (--c-gold, --c-obsidian, Cormorant Garamond font, backdrop blur, gradient buttons) is fully defined in style.css. It just isn't rendering because the pages that should show data are calling broken composable stubs. Wire the pages → design appears automatically.
🔧 BE Fixes — Exact code for every fix: remove duplicate using, fix enum, fix JWT role, add StartServingCommand, implement all AddAsync()/UpdateAsync() no-ops, add GetAllAsync() for every dead repo.
🖥 FE Fixes — Fix StaffWorkspacePage.vue with a loaders map replacing the crashed api[source].list(), fix StaffLoginPage wrong method name, fix StaffDashboardPage to call real services, fix StaffOrderDetailPage crash.
🌱 Seed Script — Complete 17_Seed.sql with IF NOT EXISTS guards for categories, 3 FB items, warehouse rows, 5 tables, 2 staff accounts, 1 customer, and PROMO10 discount code. Instructions for generating real BCrypt hashes.
✅ Checklist — 71 items across 8 phases, interactive checkboxes + progress bar. Phase 1 takes ~15 minutes and unblocks everything else.
